

# Dahua

## Wired

### IPC-Color-4k-T



<details>
  <summary>Click me to reveal full comprehensive list of API endpoints</summary>

The full list of API commands for this particular camera (Dahua Web5 interface) can be accessed by the following endpoint:
`http://admin:Password@<ip_address>/cgi-bin/configManager.cgi?action=getConfig&name=All`
Which in turn can be easily accessed on most computers via:
`curl --digest -u <username>:<password> -L "http://<username>:<password>@<ip_address>/cgi-bin/configManager.cgi?action=getConfig&name=All"`
Changing <username>, <password>, and <ip_address> where necessary.

<details>
  <summary>Click me to reveal a list of noteworthy API endpoints</summary>

The white lights on this device can be manually changed via the following commands:

```
Set off:
curl --digest -u admin:Password -L --globoff "http://admin:Password@192.168.10.30/cgi-bin/configManager.cgi?action=setConfig&Lighting_V2[0][0][0].Mode=Off"

Set Manual:
curl --digest -u admin:Password -L --globoff "http://admin:Password@192.168.10.30/cgi-bin/configManager.cgi?action=setConfig&Lighting_V2[0][0][0].Mode=Manual"

Set Auto:
curl --digest -u admin:Password -L --globoff "http://admin:Password@192.168.10.30/cgi-bin/configManager.cgi?action=setConfig&Lighting_V2[0][0][0].Mode=Auto"
```
Note that these changes are made on a per-profile basis (eg Day, Night, General, Front Light, etc), and the desired profile is specified by targeting the index for it in the middle value.  Eg: Day is first and indexing starts with 0, so [0][0][0] is Day.  [0][1][0] is Night, [0][2][0] is General, etc.  





</details>
